## Legend

* Context: either `main` for the Maven `src/man` folder or `test` for `src/test`
* File count: affected files
* File bytes: the total number of bytes of the affected files
* Lines total: the total number of lines read
* Lines empty: the number of lines containing no characters or only whitespace characters
* Lines empty %: the percentage of empty lines on the total lines
* Chars total: the total number of characters read (assuming Windows line ending)
* Chars WS: the number of whitespace characters read (excluding line ending)
* Chars WS %: the percentage of whitespace characters on the total characters

### File types

* Batch/Shell files
    * Extensions: `.bat, .cmd, .sh`
    * Charset: `ISO-8859-1`
* Code generation files
    * Extensions: `.jj, .jjt`
    * Charset: `UTF-8`
* Code list files
    * Extensions: `.cva, .gc`
    * Charset: `UTF-8`
* CSS files
    * Extensions: `.css, .scss`
    * Charset: `UTF-8`
* CSV files
    * Extensions: `.csv`
    * Charset: `UTF-8`
* git files
    * Extensions: `.gitignore`
    * Charset: `UTF-8`
* Groovy files
    * Extensions: `.groovy`
    * Charset: `UTF-8`
* HTML files
    * Extensions: `.htm, .html, .xhtml`
    * Charset: `UTF-8`
* Java files
    * Extensions: `.java, .jsp`
    * Charset: `UTF-8`
* JDM files
    * Extensions: `.jdm`
    * Charset: `UTF-8`
* JavaScript files
    * Extensions: `.js`
    * Charset: `UTF-8`
* JSON files
    * Extensions: `.json`
    * Charset: `UTF-8`
* Properties files
    * Extensions: `.conf, .properties, .properties_`
    * Charset: `UTF-8`
* RelaxNG files
    * Extensions: `.rnc, .rng`
    * Charset: `UTF-8`
* SQL files
    * Extensions: `.sql`
    * Charset: `UTF-8`
* Text files
    * Extensions: `.md, .text, .txt`
    * Charset: `UTF-8`
* XML files
    * Extensions: `.dita, .dtd, .gc_, .isdoc, .jrxml, .sch, .scmt, .status, .svrl, .ves, .wsdl, .xjb, .xjc, .xml, .xq, .xsd, .xsig, .xsl, .xslt`
    * Charset: `UTF-8`
* Excel files
    * Extensions: `.ods, .xls, .xlsx`
    * Charset: `UTF-8`
* Flash files
    * Extensions: `.swf`
    * Charset: `UTF-8`
* Font files
    * Extensions: `.eot, .ttf`
    * Charset: `UTF-8`
* Image files
    * Extensions: `.bmp, .gif, .icc, .ico, .jpg, .otf, .png, .svg, .woff, .woff2`
    * Charset: `UTF-8`
* Keystore files
    * Extensions: `.bks, .cer, .cert, .crt, .der, .jks, .keystore, .p12, .pem, .pfx`
    * Charset: `UTF-8`
* PDF files
    * Extensions: `.pdf`
    * Charset: `UTF-8`
* RAR files
    * Extensions: `.rar`
    * Charset: `UTF-8`
* Word files
    * Extensions: `.doc, .docx, .odt`
    * Charset: `UTF-8`
* ZIP files
    * Extensions: `.asice, .gz, .zip`
    * Charset: `UTF-8`
* Known other files
    * Extensions: `.95, .as4in, .attachment, .b64, .bak, .cat, .dat, .decrypted, .diff, .ent, .episode, .flow, .header, .ijmap, .in, .inc, .incl, .interface, .map, .mapping, .md5, .mime, .mmd, .mod, .pac, .payload, .rxg, .rxm, .sha256, .template, .types`
    * Charset: `UTF-8`
* Unknown other files
    * Extensions: *anything else*
    * Charset: `UTF-8`

---

My personal [Coding Styleguide](https://github.com/phax/meta/blob/master/CodingStyleguide.md) |
It is appreciated if you star the GitHub project if you like it.
